	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Bernardo Silva</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>

		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For the Portuguese Olympic sailor, see <a href="/wiki/Bernardo_Silva_(sailor)" title="Bernardo Silva (sailor)">Bernardo Silva (sailor)</a>.</div>
<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Portuguese footballer</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This name uses <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_name" title="Portuguese name">Portuguese naming customs</a>: the first or maternal <a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">family name</a> is <i>Mota Veiga</i>&#32;and the second or paternal family name is <i>Carvalho e Silva</i>.</div>

<p><b>Bernardo Mota Veiga de Carvalho e Silva</b> (born 10 August 1994), known as <b>Bernardo Silva</b> (<span style="font-size:85%;">Portuguese pronunciation:&#160;</span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Portuguese" title="Help:IPA/Portuguese">[bnadu siv]</a></span>) or simply <b>Bernardo</b>, is a Portuguese professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielder</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal national team</a>.
</p><p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Lisbon" title="Lisbon">Lisbon</a>, Silva came through <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica" title="S.L. Benfica">Benfica</a>'s youth academy. He began playing for <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica_B" title="S.L. Benfica B">Benfica B</a> in 2013 and was promoted to the first-team in 2014, playing a few minutes with the latter. He was on loan at the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> side <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco" class="mw-redirect" title="AS Monaco">Monaco</a> during the 2014–15 season, with <i>Les Monégasques</i> making the move permanent in winter 2015. After winning the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Ligue_1_champions" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Ligue 1 champions">national championship</a> with them in 2017, he was signed by English club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester City">Manchester City</a> for a reported fee of £43.5 million. He subsequently won the Premier League and <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Manchester City F.C. season">his first season</a> in England, following this up with a <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">domestic treble</a> <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2018–19 Manchester City F.C. season">the following season</a>. He had a significant role in City becoming the first men's team in England to win a domestic treble, being named <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City#Player_of_the_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester City">Manchester City's Player of the Year</a> in 2019 and being part of the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Premier League Team of the Year</a>. Afterwards, Silva was listed among the 30-man shortlist for the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a>.
</p><p>Silva made his senior debut for Portugal in 2015 after previously being <a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">capped</a> by the nations's youth teams at <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_under-19_football_team" title="Portugal national under-19 football team">under-19</a> and <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_under-21_football_team" title="Portugal national under-21 football team">under-21</a> levels. He was chosen in Portugal's squads for the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2017 FIFA Confederations Cup">2017 Confederations Cup</a>, <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Nations_League_Finals" title="2019 UEFA Nations League Finals">2019 UEFA Nations League Finals</a> on home soil, winning the latter tournament, while also being named as the Player of the Tournament.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Benfica">Benfica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Benfica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A product of <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica" title="S.L. Benfica">S.L. Benfica</a>'s youth system, Silva played for its ranks, and in 2013 they won the 2012–13 <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Nacional_de_Juniores" title="Campeonato Nacional de Juniores">Portuguese Juniors Championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut for <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica_B" title="S.L. Benfica B">Benfica B</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Segunda_Liga" class="mw-redirect" title="Segunda Liga">Segunda Liga</a> match against <a href="/wiki/C.D._Trofense" title="C.D. Trofense">Trofense</a> on 10 August 2013 (Matchday 1).<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 October 2013, Silva made his debut for Benfica at the age of 19, in a <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Ta%C3%A7a_de_Portugal" title="2013–14 Taça de Portugal">2013–14 Taça de Portugal</a> third round 1–0 away victory against <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_de_Portugal_(league)" title="Campeonato de Portugal (league)">Campeonato Nacional de Seniores</a> club C.D. Cinfães, coming out of the bench in the 80th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> His good performance for Benfica B in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Segunda_Liga" title="2013–14 Segunda Liga">2013–14 Segunda Liga</a> earned him the league's Breakthrough Player of the Year award.<sup id="cite_ref-breakthrough_award_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-breakthrough_award-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> He was a member of Benfica's domestic <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a>-winning team of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_S.L._Benfica_season" title="2013–14 S.L. Benfica season">2013–14 season</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Monaco">Monaco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Monaco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CSKA-Monaco_(4).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/CSKA-Monaco_%284%29.jpg/220px-CSKA-Monaco_%284%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="322" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/CSKA-Monaco_%284%29.jpg/330px-CSKA-Monaco_%284%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/CSKA-Monaco_%284%29.jpg/440px-CSKA-Monaco_%284%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="624" data-file-height="912" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CSKA-Monaco_(4).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Bernardo Silva playing for Monaco in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">2016–17 Champions League</a></div></div></div>
<p>On 7 August 2014, Silva joined <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> on one-year loan deal.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut on 17 August in a Ligue 1 away match against <a href="/wiki/Girondins_de_Bordeaux" class="mw-redirect" title="Girondins de Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Lucas_Ocampos" title="Lucas Ocampos">Lucas Ocampos</a> in the second half.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> On 21 September, he made his first start, in a 1–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/En_Avant_de_Guingamp" class="mw-redirect" title="En Avant de Guingamp">Guingamp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> On 14 December, he scored the only goal of a home win against <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>.
</p><p>On 20 January 2015, Benfica announced that Silva's economic and sports rights had been sold to Monaco for €15.75 million;<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> he signed a contract for Monaco that would expire on 30 June 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> On 10 April, he scored twice in a 3–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> On 10 August 2015, Silva extended his contract by one year, tying him to the club until June 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League group stage">2016–17 Champions League group stage</a> away match against <a href="/wiki/PFC_CSKA_Moscow" title="PFC CSKA Moscow">CSKA Moscow</a> on 18 October 2016, Silva scored Monaco's equalizer in the 87th minute to ensure that the match finished in 1–1 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> On 15 January 2017, he scored Monaco's last two goals in a 4–1 away win over Marseille to help Monaco move to the top of the Ligue 1 table for the first time since Week 5 of the current Ligue 1 season.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> The following 29 January, Silva scored an added-time equaliser in the 1–1 draw against reigning league champions <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a>, putting his team on top of the league.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He finished the 2016–17 season with 8 goals and 9 <a href="/wiki/Assist_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Assist (football)">assists</a> in the league and 11 goals and 12 assists in 58 matches across all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_City">Manchester City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Manchester City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2017–18 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The calibre of his performances against Manchester City for Monaco in the UEFA Champions League knockout legs in the 2016–17 season was noted by head coach <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> and his backroom staff.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> On 26 May 2017, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester City F.C">Manchester City</a> confirmed the signing of Silva on a five-year contract after passing his medical tests. Although the transfer fee remains undisclosed, it has been reported to amount to €50 million (£43.5 million), which could reach €70 million with add-ons.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva officially joined the club on 1 July 2017, ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Manchester City F.C. season">2017–18 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 February 2018, Silva scored his first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> goal for the City in a 4–0 away victory against <a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">Basel</a> in the first leg of the round of 16 stage.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 5 March, Silva scored the solitary winning goal against Chelsea at home – a key win which put them only three wins away from winning the Premier League title.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> He established himself as a consistent performer, playing the most matches of any City player in the season up to the end of February 2018. By the end of the season, he had played for Manchester City 53 times in all competitions – the most of any City player that season<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and helped them to a record 100 points in the Premier League and the EFL Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2018–19 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Silva made 51 appearances for Manchester City during the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2018–19 Manchester City F.C. season">2018–19 season</a>, scoring 13 goals and adding 14 assists in all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 24 April 2019, Silva scored the opening goal for City against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_Derby" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester Derby">Manchester Derby</a>, and the 2–0 win at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> put his team on top of the league.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva's consistent and influential performances helped his team to win Premier League title, filling in <a href="/wiki/Kevin_De_Bruyne" title="Kevin De Bruyne">Kevin De Bruyne</a>'s position who missed the majority of the season with an injury. As a result, he was voted into the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> alongside four other City players<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> and won the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C.#Player_of_the_Year" title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City Player of the Season</a> award, voted by the fans.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2019–20 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2019–20 Manchester City F.C. season">2019–20 season</a>, Silva scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in an 8–0 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League" title="2019–20 Premier League">Premier League</a> on 21 September.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Days later, he was accused of <a href="/wiki/Racism_in_association_football" title="Racism in association football">being racist</a> towards his teammate <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Mendy" title="Benjamin Mendy">Benjamin Mendy</a> in a tweet which likened the player's appearance to that of a dark-skinned advertising mascot;<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Mendy said that he was not offended.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> In November, Silva was banned for one match and fined £50,000 for the tweet.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In October 2019, Silva was nominated as one amongst 30 candidates for Ballon d´Or.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 10 January 2021, Silva scored a brace in a 3–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/EFL_Championship" title="EFL Championship">Championship</a> side <a href="/wiki/Birmingham_City_F.C." title="Birmingham City F.C.">Birmingham City</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_FA_Cup" title="2020–21 FA Cup">Third Round</a> of the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> On 20 January 2021, Silva scored his first league goal of the season in a 2–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On 24 February 2021, Silva scored his first Champions League goal of the season in a 2–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a> in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Round_of_16" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">round of 16</a> tie.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:New_Zealand-Portugal_(8).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/New_Zealand-Portugal_%288%29.jpg/170px-New_Zealand-Portugal_%288%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="241" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/New_Zealand-Portugal_%288%29.jpg/255px-New_Zealand-Portugal_%288%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/New_Zealand-Portugal_%288%29.jpg/340px-New_Zealand-Portugal_%288%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="609" data-file-height="865" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:New_Zealand-Portugal_(8).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva at the <a href="/wiki/2017_Confederations_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="2017 Confederations Cup">2017 Confederations Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>In 2013, Silva represented Portugal at the <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2013 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2013 European Under-19 Championship</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> reaching the semi-finals. For his performances, he was named among the top 10 talents under the age of 19 in Europe by a selection of <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> reporters.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 March 2015, Silva made his senior debut for <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a>, starting in a 0–2 friendly defeat to <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde_national_football_team" title="Cape Verde national football team">Cape Verde</a> in <a href="/wiki/Estoril" title="Estoril">Estoril</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 June 2015, Silva scored <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_under-21_football_team" title="Portugal national under-21 football team">Portugal U21s</a>' first goal in a 5–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_under-21_football_team" title="Germany national under-21 football team">Germany U21</a> in the semi-finals of the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2015 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">European Under-21 Championship</a> in Czech Republic.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> He was left out of the Portuguese squad for the finals of <a href="/wiki/Euro_2016" class="mw-redirect" title="Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a> due to injury.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was selected for the Portugal squad for the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2017 FIFA Confederations Cup">2017 Confederations Cup</a> which was hosted in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. He scored the second goal of the match in the group stage of the tournament, a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_national_football_team" title="New Zealand national football team">New Zealand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> The national team reached the semi-finals before losing out to <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shootout</a> after a 0–0 draw at the end of regulation time. He missed the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_knockout_stage#Third_place_play-off" title="2017 FIFA Confederations Cup knockout stage">third place play-off</a> in which Portugal defeated <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a> 2–1 after extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was named in Portugal's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> He featured in all 4 matches with Portugal, but was knocked out of the tournament after a 1–2 loss to Uruguay.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was selected for three matches in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Nations League">2018–19 UEFA Nations League</a> group stage, scoring a goal in a 3–2 victory against <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_football_team" title="Poland national football team">Poland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Nations_League_Finals" title="2019 UEFA Nations League Finals">UEFA Nations League Finals</a>, Silva played both matches and registered an assist in each as Portugal won the trophy, and was named the tournament's best player.<sup id="cite_ref-unl_pot_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unl_pot-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Silva is a diminutive, elegant, and creative left-footed <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a>, with a slender build, who is capable of playing in several attacking and midfield positions. Throughout his career, he has been fielded in a variety of roles, including as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> on either flank (although he favours the right side of the pitch), as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deep-lying playmaker</a>, as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>, or even as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">second striker</a>; he has also been deployed in a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#False-9" title="Forward (association football)">false-9</a> role, or even as <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Wing-back" title="Defender (association football)">wing-back</a> on occasion. He is mainly known for his technique, acceleration, agility, passing, vision, and <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills, as well as his energy and defensive work-rate, which enables him to cover ground, press opponents, and start attacks after winning back possession. Although he is known for his ability to carry the ball forward, run at defences, and retain possession, he is also known to be an intelligent team player, with a strong personality, who prefers to participate in the build-up of offensive plays rather than undertaking individual dribbling runs. Despite primarily being a creative midfielder, he is also capable of scoring goals himself.<sup id="cite_ref-2019_Ballon_d&#39;Or_Rankings_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019_Ballon_d&#39;Or_Rankings-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bernardo_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Silva is a supporter of Portuguese club S.L. Benfica.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> His English has been described as "perfect" by the media,<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> partly as a result of his parents sending him to an English-speaking school in Lisbon when he was six years old.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Silva's cousin <a href="/wiki/Matilde_Fidalgo" title="Matilde Fidalgo">Matilde Fidalgo</a>, also born in 1994, has represented <a href="/wiki/Portugal_women%27s_national_football_team" title="Portugal women&#39;s national football team">Portugal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_W.F.C." title="Manchester City W.F.C.">Manchester City</a>'s women's teams.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
